## USER 🧑‍💻

- 祝日データを作成・修正・削除できるようにフロントエンドのメニューと form 、バックエンドの API を追加
- form においては、年を切り替えることで一度に表示する祝日データを制限する
- form の初期表示は、選択した年の祝日一覧とし、一覧から、追加・修正・削除へ遷移できる。
- Nager.Date から、祝日をインポートできる
  - インターネットに接続できない環境では、Nager.Date から取得した JSON をインポートできる

---

  }

(error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch holidays' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 祝日作成 (ADMIN のみ)\napp.post('/api/holidays', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== 'ADMIN') return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });\n  const { name, date, start, end } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const holiday = await prisma.holiday.create({\n      data: { name, date, start, end }\n    });\n    res.json(holiday);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to create holiday' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 祝日更新 (ADMIN のみ)\napp.put('/api/holidays/:id', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== 'ADMIN') return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });\n  const { id } = req.params;\n  const { name, date, start, end } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const holiday = await prisma.holiday.update({\n      where: { id },\n      data: { name, date, start, end }\n    });\n    res.json(holiday);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update holiday' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 祝日削除 (ADMIN のみ)\napp.delete('/api/holidays/:id', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== 'ADMIN') return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });\n  const { id } = req.params;\n  try {\n    await prisma.holiday.delete({ where: { id } });\n    res.json({ message: 'Holiday deleted successfully' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to delete holiday' });\n  }\n});\n\n// Nager.Date からのインポート (ADMIN のみ)\napp.post('/api/holidays/import-nager', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== 'ADMIN') return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });\n  const { year, countryCode } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const response = await fetch(`https://date.nager.at/api/v3/PublicHolidays/${year}/${countryCode}`);\n    if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Nager.Date API failed');\n    const nagerHolidays: any[] = await response.json();\n    \n    const holidays = await Promise.all(nagerHolidays.map(nh => \n      prisma.holiday.create({\n        data: {\n          name: nh.localName || nh.name,\n          date: nh.date\n        }\n      })\n    ));\n    res.json(holidays);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to import holidays from Nager.Date' });\n  }\n});\n\n// JSON ファイルからのインポート (ADMIN のみ)\napp.post('/api/holidays/import-json', verifyToken, async (req, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== 'ADMIN') return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Forbidden' });\n  const { holidays: nagerHolidays } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const holidays = await Promise.all(nagerHolidays.map((nh: any) => \n      prisma.holiday.create({\n        data: {\n          name: nh.localName || nh.name,\n          date: nh.date\n        }\n      })\n    ));\n    res.json(holidays);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to import holidays from JSON' });\n  }\n});",
    "file_path": "backend/src/index.ts",

## MODEL ✨

I will create `src/components/HolidayManager.tsx`, using `RoomManager.tsx` as a reference. The component will include functionality for filtering by year, managing holidays (Add/Edit/Delete), and importing from Nager.Date or a local JSON file.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "read_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/components/RoomManager.tsx"
  }
}
```

## USER 🧑‍💻

```json

  "id": "read_file_1775298708523_0",
  "name": "read_file",
  "response": {
    "output": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { Resource, ResourceLabels } from '../types';\nimport './RoomManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onUpdate: () => void;\n  resources: Resource[];\n  labels: ResourceLabels;\n}\n\nexport function {\n    if (!formData.name) {\n      alert(t('Please enter a name'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/rooms`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n        },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          id: selectedRoomId,\n          ...formData\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save room'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving room:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async () => {\n    if (!selectedRoomId) return;\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this room?'))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/rooms/${selectedRoomId}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to delete room'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting room:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"room-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"room-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"room-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage {{resource}}', { resource: labels.room })}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"room-manager-content\">\n          <div className=\"room-selector\">\n            <label>{t('Select {{resource}} to Edit', { resource: labels.room })}</label>\n            <select \n              value={selectedRoomId || ''} \n              onChange={(e) => setSelectedRoomId(e.currentTarget.value || null)}\n            >\n              <option value=\"\">{t('Add New {{resource}}', { resource: labels.room })}</option>\n              {rooms.map(r => (\n                <option key={r.id} value={r.id}>{r.name}</option>\n              ))}\n            </select>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"room-form\">\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('{{resource}} Name', { resource: labels.room })}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"text\" \n                value={formData.name} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, name: e.currentTarget.value })}\n              />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Order')}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"number\" \n                value={formData.order} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, order: parseInt(e.currentTarget.value) || 0 })}\n              />\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"room-manager-footer\">\n          {selectedRoomId && (\n            <button className=\"delete-button\" onClick={handleDelete}>{t('Delete')}</button>\n          )}\n          <div className=\"footer-right\">\n            <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n            <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleSave}>{t('Save Changes')}</button>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I will create `src/components/HolidayManager.tsx`, incorporating a year filter for the holiday list based on `date` or `start` year. I'll also implement a year-selectable Nager.Date import and a file input for local JSON imports, sending the data to the backend.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { Holiday } from '../types';\nimport { parseISO, getYear } from 'date-fns';\nimport './HolidayManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onUpdate: () => void;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n}\n\nexport function HolidayManager({ backendUrl, onClose, onUpdate, holidays }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [selectedYear, setSelectedYear] = useState<number>(new Date().getFullYear());\n  const [editingHolidayId, setEditingHolidayId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<Partial<Holiday>>({\n    name: '',\n    date: '',\n    start: '',\n    end: ''\n  });\n  const [isImportMode, setIsImportMode] = useState<boolean>(false);\n  const [importYear, setImportYear] = useState<number>(new Date().getFullYear());\n  const [countryCode, setCountryCode] = useState<string>('JP');\n\n  const years = Array.from(new Set(holidays.map(h => {\n    const d = h.date || h.start;\n    return d ? getYear(parseISO(d)) : null;\n  }).filter(y => y !== null))) as number[];\n  \n  if (!years.includes(new Date().getFullYear())) {\n    years.push(new Date().getFullYear());\n  }\n  years.sort((a, b) => b - a);\n\n  const filteredHolidays = holidays.filter(h => {\n    const d = h.date || h.start;\n    return d && getYear(parseISO(d)) === selectedYear;\n  }).sort((a, b) => (a.date || a.start || '').localeCompare(b.date || b.start || ''));\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (editingHolidayId) {\n      const holiday = holidays.find(h => h.id === editingHolidayId);\n      if (holiday) {\n        setFormData(holiday);\n      }\n    } else {\n      setFormData({\n        name: '',\n        date: '',\n        start: '',\n        end: ''\n      });\n    }\n  }, [editingHolidayId, holidays]);\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    if (!formData.name || (!formData.date && (!formData.start || !formData.end))) {\n      alert(t('Please enter a name and date/range'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const url = editingHolidayId ? `${backendUrl}/holidays/${editingHolidayId}` : `${backendUrl}/holidays`;\n      const method = editingHolidayId ? 'PUT' : 'POST';\n      const res = await fetch(url, {\n        method,\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify(formData)\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        setEditingHolidayId(null);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save holiday'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving holiday:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this holiday?'))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/holidays/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to delete holiday'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting holiday:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleImportNager = async () => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Import holidays for {{year}} from Nager.Date?', { year: importYear }))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/holidays/import-nager`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ year: importYear, countryCode })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        setIsImportMode(false);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to import holidays'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error importing holidays:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleImportJson = async (e: any) => {\n    const file = e.target.files?.[0];\n    if (!file) return;\n\n    const reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onload = async (event) => {\n      try {\n        const json = JSON.parse(event.target?.result as string);\n        const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/holidays/import-json`, {\n          method: 'POST',\n          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n          credentials: 'include',\n          body: JSON.stringify({ holidays: json })\n        });\n        if (res.ok) {\n          onUpdate();\n          setIsImportMode(false);\n        } else {\n          alert(t('Failed to import holidays from JSON'));\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error parsing JSON:', err);\n        alert(t('Invalid JSON file'));\n      }\n    };\n    reader.readAsText(file);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"holiday-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"holiday-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"holiday-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage Holidays')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"holiday-manager-content\">\n          {!isImportMode && !editingHolidayId && (\n            <>\n              <div className=\"year-selector\">\n                <label>{t('Year')}</label>\n                <select value={selectedYear} onChange={(e) => setSelectedYear(parseInt(e.currentTarget.value))}>\n                  {years.map(y => <option key={y} value={y}>{y}</option>)}\n                </select>\n                <div className=\"header-actions\">\n                  <button onClick={() => setEditingHolidayId('new')}>{t('Add Holiday')}</button>\n                  <button onClick={() => setIsImportMode(true)}>{t('Import')}</button>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"holiday-list\">\n                <table>\n                  <thead>\n                    <tr>\n                      <th>{t('Date')}</th>\n                      <th>{t('Name')}</th>\n                      <th>{t('Actions')}</th>\n                    </tr>\n                  </thead>\n                  <tbody>\n                    {filteredHolidays.map(h => (\n                      <tr key={h.id}>\n                        <td>{h.date || `${h.start} ~ ${h.end}`}</td>\n                        <td>{h.name}</td>\n                        <td>\n                          <button onClick={() => setEditingHolidayId(h.id)}>{t('Edit')}</button>\n                          <button className=\"delete-btn\" onClick={() => handleDelete(h.id)}>{t('Delete')}</button>\n                        </td>\n                      </tr>\n                    ))}\n                    {filteredHolidays.length === 0 && (\n                      <tr>\n                        <td colSpan={3} className=\"empty-message\">{t('No holidays found for this year')}</td>\n                      </tr>\n                    )}\n                  </tbody>\n                </table>\n              </div>\n            </>\n          )}\n\n          {editingHolidayId && (\n            <div className=\"holiday-form\">\n              <h3>{editingHolidayId === 'new' ? t('Add Holiday') : t('Edit Holiday')}</h3>\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('Holiday Name')}</label>\n                <input \n                  type=\"text\" \n                  value={formData.name} \n                  onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, name: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                />\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"form-row\">\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Single Date')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"date\" \n                    value={formData.date || ''} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, date: e.currentTarget.value, start: '', end: '' })}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"form-row\">\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Start Date (for range)')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"date\" \n                    value={formData.start || ''} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, start: e.currentTarget.value, date: '' })}\n                  />\n                </div>\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('End Date (for range)')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"date\" \n                    value={formData.end || ''} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, end: e.currentTarget.value, date: '' })}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"form-actions\">\n                <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={() => setEditingHolidayId(null)}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n                <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleSave}>{t('Save')}</button>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n\n          {isImportMode && (\n            <div className=\"import-section\">\n              <h3>{t('Import Holidays')}</h3>\n              <div className=\"import-nager\">\n                <h4>Nager.Date API</h4>\n                <div className=\"form-row\">\n                  <div className=\"form-group\">\n                    <label>{t('Year')}</label>\n                    <input \n                      type=\"number\" \n                      value={importYear} \n                      onInput={(e) => setImportYear(parseInt(e.currentTarget.value))}\n                    />\n                  </div>\n                  <div className=\"form-group\">\n                    <label>{t('Country Code')}</label>\n                    <input \n                      type=\"text\" \n                      value={countryCode} \n                      onInput={(e) => setCountryCode(e.currentTarget.value.toUpperCase())}\n                    />\n                  </div>\n                </div>\n                <button onClick={handleImportNager}>{t('Import from Nager.Date')}</button>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"import-json\">\n                <h4>{t('Local JSON File')}</h4>\n                <p>{t('Select a JSON file downloaded from Nager.Date')}</p>\n                <input type=\"file\" accept=\".json\" onChange={handleImportJson} />\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"form-actions\">\n                <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={() => setIsImportMode(false)}>{t('Back')}</button>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",
    "file_path": "src/components/HolidayManager.tsx"
  }
}

No token provided.' });\n  }\n\n  try {\n    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET) as { id: string; role: UserRole };\n    req.user = decoded;\n    next();\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid token.' });\n  }\n};\n\nexport const checkRole = (roles: UserRole[]) => {\n  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction) => {\n    if (!req.user || !roles.includes(req.user.role)) {\n      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Insufficient permissions.' });\n    }\n    next();\n  };\n};\n"

  "id": "read_file_1775363494923_0",

  "response": {
    "output": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { Holiday } from '../types';\nimport { parseISO, getYear } from 'date-fns';\nimport './HolidayManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onUpdate: () => void;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n}\n\nexport function HolidayManager({ backendUrl, onClose, onUpdate, holidays }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [selectedYear, setSelectedYear] = useState<number>(new Date().getFullYear());\n  const [editingHolidayId, setEditingHolidayId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<Partial<Holiday>>({\n    name: '',\n    date: '',\n    start: '',\n    end: ''\n  });\n  const [isImportMode, setIsImportMode] = useState<boolean>(false);\n  const [importYear, setImportYear] = useState<number>(new Date().getFullYear());\n  const [countryCode, setCountryCode] = useState<string>('JP');\n\n  const years = Array.from(new Set(holidays.map(h => {\n    const d = h.date || h.start;\n    return d ? getYear(parseISO(d)) : null;\n  }).filter(y => y !== null))) as number[];\n  \n  if (!years.includes(new Date().getFullYear())) {\n    years.push(new Date().getFullYear());\n  }\n  years.sort((a, b) => b - a);\n\n  const filteredHolidays = holidays.filter(h => {\n    const d = h.date || h.start;\n    return d && getYear(parseISO(d)) === selectedYear;\n  }).sort((a, b) => (a.date || a.start || '').localeCompare(b.date || b.start || ''));\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (editingHolidayId) {\n      const holiday = holidays.find(h => h.id === editingHolidayId);\n      if (holiday) {\n        setFormData(holiday);\n      }\n    } else {\n      setFormData({\n        name: '',\n        date: '',\n        start: '',\n        end: ''\n      });\n    }\n  }, [editingHolidayId, holidays]);\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    if (!formData.name || (!formData.date && (!formData.start || !formData.end))) {\n      alert(t('Please enter a name and date/range'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const url = editingHolidayId ? `${backendUrl}/holidays/${editingHolidayId}` : `${backendUrl}/holidays`;\n      const method = editingHolidayId ? 'PUT' : 'POST';\n      const res = await fetch(url, {\n        method,\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify(formData)\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        setEditingHolidayId(null);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save holiday'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving holiday:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async (id: string) => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this holiday?'))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/holidays/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to delete holiday'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting holiday:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleImportNager = async () => {\n    if (!confirm(t('Import holidays for {{year}} from Nager.Date?', { year: importYear }))) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/holidays/import-nager`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ year: importYear, countryCode })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        setIsImportMode(false);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to import holidays'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error importing holidays:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleImportJson = async (e: any) => {\n    const file = e.target.files?.[0];\n    if (!file) return;\n\n    const reader = new FileReader();\n    reader.onload = async (event) => {\n      try {\n        const json = JSON.parse(event.target?.result as string);\n        const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/holidays/import-json`, {\n          method: 'POST',\n          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n          credentials: 'include',\n          body: JSON.stringify({ holidays: json })\n        });\n        if (res.ok) {\n          onUpdate();\n          setIsImportMode(false);\n        } else {\n          alert(t('Failed to import holidays from JSON'));\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Error parsing JSON:', err);\n        alert(t('Invalid JSON file'));\n      }\n    };\n    reader.readAsText(file);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"holiday-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"holiday-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"holiday-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage Holidays')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"holiday-manager-content\">\n          {!isImportMode && !editingHolidayId && (\n            <>\n              <div className=\"year-selector\">\n                <label>{t('Year')}</label>\n                <select value={selectedYear} onChange={(e) => setSelectedYear(parseInt(e.currentTarget.value))}>\n                  {years.map(y => <option key={y} value={y}>{y}</option>)}\n                </select>\n                <div className=\"header-actions\">\n                  <button onClick={() => setEditingHolidayId('new')}>{t('Add Holiday')}</button>\n                  <button onClick={() => setIsImportMode(true)}>{t('Import')}</button>\n                </div>\n              </div>\n\n              <div className=\"holiday-list\">\n                <table>\n                  <thead>\n                    <tr>\n                      <th>{t('Date')}</th>\n (\n                      <tr key={h.id}>\n                        <td>{h.date || `${h.start} ~ ${h.end}`}</td>\n                        <td>{h.name}</td>\n                        <td>\n                          <button onClick={() => setEditingHolidayId(h.id)}>{t('Edit')}</button>\n                          <button className=\"delete-btn\" onClick={() => handleDelete(h.id)}>{t('Delete')}</button>\n                        </td>\n                      </tr>\n                    ))}\n                    {filteredHolidays.length === 0 && (\n                      <tr>\n                        <td className=\"form-row\">\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Single Date')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"date\" \n                    value={formData.date || ''} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, date: e.currentTarget.value, start: '', end: '' })}\n                  />\n                </div>\n ## USER 🧑‍💻

祝日設定画面で年をカレンダーから選択できないか?

---

## MODEL ✨

祝日設定画面で、特定の年月日をカレンダーから選ぶことで、その年（Year）を自動的に選択状態にする機能を追加します。
また、メインのスケジュール画面で表示している日付の年を初期値として引き継ぐように修正します。

### 1. `App.tsx` の修正
メイン画面の `currentDate` から年を取得して `HolidayManager` に渡すようにします。

```tsx
// src/App.tsx の修正箇所

// ... 略 ...
      {showHolidayManager.value && (
        <HolidayManager 
          backendUrl={BACKEND_URL} 
          onClose={() => showHolidayManager.value = false}
          onUpdate={fetchData}
          holidays={holidays.value}
          initialYear={getYear(currentDate.value)} // 現在表示中の年を渡す
        />
      )}
// ... 略 ...
```

### 2. `HolidayManager.tsx` の修正
`initialYear` プロパティを追加し、年選択の部分にカレンダー（`type="date"`）からの選択機能を追加します。

**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "new_string": "interface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  onUpdate: () => void;\n  holidays: Holiday[];\n  initialYear?: number;\n}\n\nexport function HolidayManager({ backendUrl, onClose, onUpdate, holidays, initialYear }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [selectedYear, setSelectedYear] = useState<number>(initialYear || new Date().getFullYear());\n  const [editingHolidayId, setEditingHolidayId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState<Partial<Holiday>>({\n    name: '',\n    date: '',\n    start: '',\n    end: ''\n  });\n  const [isImportMode, setIsImportMode] = useState<boolean>(false);\n  const [importYear, setImportYear] = useState<number>(selectedYear);\n  const [countryCode, setCountryCode] = useState<string>('JP');\n\n  const years = Array.from(new Set(holidays.map(h => {\n    const d = h.date || h.start;\n    return d ? getYear(parseISO(d)) : null;\n  }).filter(y => y !== null))) as number[];\n  \n  if (!years.includes(new Date().getFullYear())) {\n    years.push(new Date().getFullYear());\n  }\n  if (initialYear && !years.includes(initialYear)) {\n    years.push(initialYear);\n  }\n  years.sort((a, b) => b - JSON.stringify(formData)\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        onUpdate();\n        setEditingHolidayId(null);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save holiday'));\n      }\n    } catch email: 'admin@example.com',\n      password: adminPassword,\n      role: UserRole.ADMIN\n    }\n  });\n\n  await prisma.user.create({\n    data: {\n      email: 'teacher@example.com',\n      password: teacherPassword,\n      role: UserRole.TEACHER\n    }\n  });\n\n  console.log('Seeding users...');\n\n  // 時限の生成\n  const periods = [\n    { id: 'p1', name: '1st Period', startTime: '09:00', endTime: '09:50', order: 1 },\n    { id: 'p2', name: '2nd Period', startTime: '10:00', endTime: '10:50', order: 2 },\n    { id: 'p3', name: '3rd Period', startTime: '11:00', endTime: '11:50', order: 3 },\n    { id: 'p4', name: '4th Period', startTime: '12:00', endTime: '12:50', order: 4 },\n    { id: 'p5', name: '5th Period', startTime: '13:50', endTime: '14:40', order: 5 },\n    { id: 'p6', name: '6th Period', startTime: '14:50', endTime: '15:40', order: 6 },\n    { id: 'p7', name: '7th Period', startTime: '15:50', endTime: '16:40', order: 7 },\n    { id: 'p8', name: '8th Period', startTime: '16:50', endTime: '17:40', order: 8 },\n  ];\n\n  for (const p of periods) {\n    await prisma.timePeriod.create({ data: p });\n  }\n\n  console.log('Seeding time periods...');\n\n  // リソースラベルの生成\n  await prisma.resourceLabel.create({\n    data: {\n      room: 'Room',\n      teacher: 'Teacher',\n      course: 'Course',\n      event: 'Event',\n      mainTeacher: 'Main Teacher',\n      subTeacher: 'Sub Teacher'\n    }\n  });\n\n  console.log('Seeding resource labels...');\n\n  // リソースの生成\n  // Rooms\n  for (let i = 1; i <= 20; i++) {\n    await prisma.resource.create({\n      data: { id: `r${i}`, name: `Room ${100 + i}`, type: 'room', order: i }\n    });\n  }\n  // Teachers\n  const surnames = ['Sato', 'Suzuki', 'Takahashi', 'Tanaka', 'Watanabe', 'Ito', 'Yamamoto', 'Nakamura', 'Kobayashi', 'Kato', 'Yoshida', 'Yamada', 'Sasaki', 'Yamaguchi', 'Matsumoto', 'Inoue', 'Kimura', 'Hayashi', 'Saito', 'Shimizu'];\n  for (let i = 1; i <= 20; i++) {\n    await prisma.resource.create({\n      data: { \n        id: `t${i}`, \n        name: `Dr. ${surnames[i-1]}`, \n        type: 'teacher', \n        order: i,\n        // 佐藤先生 (t1) だけユーザーと紐付け\n        userId: i === 1 ? userT1.id : undefined\n      }\n    });\n  }\n  // Courses\n  const courseNames = ['Advanced Math', 'Practical English', 'Physics Inquiry', 'Japanese History B', 'Modern Writing', 'Basic Chemistry', 'World History A', 'Geography B', 'Biology Special', 'Politics & Economy', 'Classical Literature', 'Informatics I', 'Basic Arts', 'Physical Education', 'English Expression', 'Math IIB', 'Logical Japanese', 'Human Science', 'Career Inquiry', 'Multiculturalism'];\n  for (let i = 1; i <= 20; i++) {\n    await prisma.resource.create({\n      data: { id: `c${i}`, name: `${courseNames[i-1]} Course`, type: 'course', order: i }\n    });\n  }\n\n  console.log('Seeding resources...');\n\n  // 授業の生成\n  const subjects = ['Math', 'English', 'Physics', 'Japanese', 'Chemistry', 'History', 'Geography', 'Biology', 'Social', 'Info', 'Arts', 'PE'];\n  const baseDate = '2026-03-26';\n\n  for (let i = 1; i <= 20; i++) {\n    const periodNum = (i % 8) + 1;\n    await prisma.lesson.create({\n      data: {\n        subject: subjects[i % subjects.length],\n        teacherId: `t${(i % 20) + 1}`,\n        roomId: `r${(i % 20) + 1}`,\n        courseId: `c${(i % 20) + 1}`,\n        startDate: baseDate,\n        startPeriodId: `p${periodNum}`,\n        endDate: baseDate,\n        endPeriodId: `p${periodNum}`\n      }\n    });\n  }\n\n  // 複数サブ講師のテストデータ\n  await prisma.lesson.create({\n    data: {\n      subject: 'Team Teaching: Research',\n      teacherId: 't1', // Dr. Sato\n      subTeachers: {\n        connect: [{ id: 't2' }, { id: 't3' }] // Dr. Suzuki, Dr. Takahashi\n      },\n      roomId: 'r1',\n      courseId: 'c1',\n      startDate: '2026-03-26',\n      startPeriodId: 'p3',\n      endDate: '2026-03-26',\n      endPeriodId: 'p4'\n    }\n  });\n\n  // 日を跨ぐ集中講義\n  await prisma.lesson.create({\n    data: {\n      subject: 'Special: Multiculturalism',\n      teacherId: 't5',\n      subTeachers: {\n        connect: [{ id: 't1' }, { id: 't2' }]\n      },\n      roomId: 'r5',\n      courseId: 'c20',\n      startDate: '2026-03-26',\n      startPeriodId: 'p1',\n      endDate: '2026-03-27',\n      endPeriodId: 'p4'\n    }\n  });\n\n  console.log('Seeding lessons...');\n\n  // イベント\n  // 全体イベント\n  await prisma.scheduleEvent.create({\n    data: {\n      name: 'Evacuation Drill',\n      startDate: '2026-03-26',\n      startPeriodId: 'p5',\n      endDate: '2026-03-26',\n      endPeriodId: 'p6',\n      color: '#fee2e2',\n      showInEventRow: true\n    }\n  });\n\n  // リソース固有（加藤先生のみ、イベント行なし）\n  await prisma.scheduleEvent.create({\n    data: {\n      name: 'Business Trip',\n      startDate: '2026-03-26',\n      startPeriodId: 'p1',\n      endDate: '2026-03-26',\n      endPeriodId: 'p8',\n      color: '#d1fae5',\n      showInEventRow: false,\n      resources: {\n        connect: [{ id: 't10' }]\n      }\n    }\n  });\n\n  // 両方（田中先生、104号室、イベント行あり）\n  await prisma.scheduleEvent.create({\n    data: {\n      name: 'Open Research Lesson',\n      startDate: '2026-03-26',\n      startPeriodId: 'p2',\n      endDate: '2026-03-26',\n      endPeriodId: 'p3',\n      color: '#fef3c7',\n      showInEventRow: true,\n      resources: {\n        connect: [{ id: 't4' }, { id: 'r4' }]\n      }\n    }\n  });\n\n  // その他既存のイベント\n  await prisma.scheduleEvent.create({\n    data: { name: 'School Cleaning', startDate: '2026-03-26', startPeriodId: 'p7', endDate: '2026-03-26', endPeriodId: 'p8', color: '#e2e8f0', showInEventRow: true }\n  });\n\n  // 祝日\n  await prisma.holiday.createMany({\n    data: [\n      { date: '2026-01-01', name: 'New Year\\'s Day' },\n      { date: '2026-02-11', name: 'Foundation Day' },\n      { date: '2026-02-23', name: 'Emperor\\'s Birthday' },\n      { date: '2026-03-20', name: 'Vernal Equinox Day' },\n      { date: '2026-04-29', name: 'Showa Day' },\n      { start: '2026-12-29', end: '2027-01-03', name: 'Winter Holidays' }\n    ]\n  });\n\n  console.log('Seeding finished.');\n}\n\nmain()\n  .catch((e) => {\n    console.error(e);\n    process.exit(1);\n  })\n  .finally(async () => {\n    await prisma.$disconnect();\n  });\n"
  }
}

    "new_string": "// ユーザー登録\napp.post('/api/auth/register', async (req, res) => {\n  const { email, password, role } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const settings = await prisma.systemSetting.findFirst();\n    if (settings && !settings.allowPublicSignup) {\n      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Public signup is disabled' });\n    }\n\n    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);\n    const user = await prisma.user.create({\n      data: {\n        email,\n        password: hashedPassword,\n        role: role || UserRole.STUDENT\n      }\n    });\n    res.json({ message: 'User created successfully', userId: user.id });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(400).json({ error: 'User already exists or invalid data' });\n  }\n});\n\n// パスワード変更 (自分自身)\napp.post('/api/auth/change-password', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  const { currentPassword, newPassword } = req.body;\n  if (!req.user) return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Not authenticated' });\n\n  try {\n    const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: req.user.id } });\n    if (!user) return res.status(404).json({ error: 'User not found' });\n\n    const isValid = await bcrypt.compare(currentPassword, user.password);\n    if (!isValid) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid current password' });\n\n    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(newPassword, 10);\n    await prisma.user.update({\n      where: { id: user.id },\n      data: { password: hashedPassword }\n    });\n    res.json({ message: 'Password changed successfully' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to change password' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ログイン",

```json
{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "backend/src/index.ts",
    "instruction": "Add User CRUD, reset password, and system settings routes.",
    "new_string": "// ユーザー一覧取得 (ADMIN権限)\napp.get('/api/users', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) {\n    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  try {\n    const users = await prisma.user.findMany({\n      select: { id: true, email: true, role: true }\n    });\n    res.json(users);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch users' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ユーザー作成・更新 (ADMIN権限)\napp.post('/api/users', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) {\n    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  const { id, email, password, role } = req.body;\n  try {\n    let user;\n    if (id) {\n      // 更新\n      const data: any = { email, role };\n      if (password) {\n        data.password = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);\n      }\n      user = await prisma.user.update({\n        where: { id },\n        data,\n        select: { id: true, email: true, role: true }\n      });\n    } else {\n      // 新規作成\n      const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);\n      user = await prisma.user.create({\n        data: { email, password: hashedPassword, role },\n        select: { id: true, email: true, role: true }\n      });\n    }\n    res.json(user);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save user' });\n  }\n});\n\n// ユーザー削除 (ADMIN権限)\napp.delete('/api/users/:id', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) {\n    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  const { id } = req.params;\n  try {\n    // 自分自身は削除できないようにする\n    if (req.user.id === id) {\n      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Cannot delete yourself' });\n    }\n    await prisma.user.delete({ where: { id } });\n    res.json({ message: 'User deleted successfully' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to delete user' });\n  }\n});\n\n// 管理者によるパスワードリセット (ADMIN権限)\napp.post('/api/users/:id/reset-password', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) {\n    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  const { id } = req.params;\n  const { newPassword } = req.body;\n  try {\n    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(newPassword, 10);\n    await prisma.user.update({\n      where: { id },\n      data: { password: hashedPassword }\n    });\n    res.json({ message: 'Password reset successfully' });\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to reset password' });\n  }\n});\n\n// システム設定取得\napp.get('/api/settings', async (req, res) => {\n  try {\n    let settings = await prisma.systemSetting.findFirst();\n    if (!settings) {\n      settings = await prisma.systemSetting.create({ data: { allowPublicSignup: true } });\n    }\n    res.json(settings);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch settings' });\n  }\n});\n\n// システム設定更新 (ADMIN権限)\napp.post('/api/settings', verifyToken, async (req: AuthRequest, res) => {\n  if (req.user?.role !== UserRole.ADMIN) {\n    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied. Admin role required.' });\n  }\n  const { allowPublicSignup } = req.body;\n  try {\n    let settings = await prisma.systemSetting.findFirst();\n    if (settings) {\n      settings = await prisma.systemSetting.update({\n        where: { id: settings.id },\n        data: { allowPublicSignup }\n      });\n    } else {\n      settings = await prisma.systemSetting.create({\n        data: { allowPublicSignup }\n      });\n    }\n    res.json(settings);\n  } catch (error) {\n    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to save settings' });\n  }\n});",

## MODEL ✨

Backend's ready. Frontend time. I'll create `UserManager.tsx` and `UserManager.css` for user management, `ProfileManager.tsx` and `ProfileManager.css` for personal password changes, and `SystemSettingManager.tsx` to toggle public signup. I'll also update `Login.tsx` to include an optional signup link. I'll start with `UserManager.tsx`.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { User, UserRole } from '../types';\nimport './UserManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  currentUser: User;\n}\n\nexport function UserManager({ backendUrl, onClose, currentUser }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [users, setUsers] = useState<User[]>([]);\n  const [selectedUserId, setSelectedUserId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({\n    email: '',\n    password: '',\n    role: 'STUDENT' as UserRole\n  });\n  const [resetPasswordMode, setResetPasswordMode] = useState(false);\n  const [newPassword, setNewPassword] = useState('');\n\n  const fetchUsers = async () => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users`, { credentials: 'include' });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        const data = await res.json();\n        setUsers(data);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to fetch users:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchUsers();\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (selectedUserId) {\n      const user = users.find(u => u.id === selectedUserId);\n      if (user) {\n        setFormData({\n          email: user.email,\n          password: '', // パスワードは表示しない\n          role: user.role\n        });\n      }\n    } else {\n      setFormData({\n        email: '',\n        password: '',\n        role: 'STUDENT'\n      });\n    }\n    setResetPasswordMode(false);\n  }, [selectedUserId, users]);\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    if (!formData.email || (!selectedUserId && !formData.password)) {\n      alert(t('Please fill in all required fields'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          id: selectedUserId,\n          ...formData\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        fetchUsers();\n        setSelectedUserId(null);\n        alert(t('User saved successfully'));\n      } else {\n        const errData = await res.json();\n        alert(errData.error || t('Failed to save user'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving user:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async () => {\n    if (!selectedUserId) return;\n    if (selectedUserId === currentUser.id) {\n      alert(t('Cannot delete yourself'));\n      return;\n    }\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this user?'))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users/${selectedUserId}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        fetchUsers();\n        setSelectedUserId(null);\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to delete user'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting user:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleResetPassword = async () => {\n    if (!selectedUserId || !newPassword) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users/${selectedUserId}/reset-password`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ newPassword })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        setResetPasswordMode(false);\n        setNewPassword('');\n        alert(t('Password reset successfully'));\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to reset password'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error resetting password:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"user-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"user-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"user-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage Users')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"user-manager-content\">\n          <div className=\"user-selector\">\n            <label>{t('Select User to Edit')}</label>\n            <select \n              value={selectedUserId || ''} \n              onChange={(e) => setSelectedUserId(e.currentTarget.value || null)}\n            >\n              <option value=\"\">{t('Add New User')}</option>\n              {users.map(u => (\n                <option key={u.id} value={u.id}>{u.email} ({u.role})</option>\n              ))}\n            </select>\n          </div>\n\n          {!resetPasswordMode ?               value={formData.email} \n                  onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, email: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                />\n              </div>\n              {!selectedUserId && (\n                <div className=\"form-group\">\n                  <label>{t('Password')}</label>\n                  <input \n                    type=\"password\" \n                    value={formData.password} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, password: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              )}\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('Role')}</label>\n                <select \n                  value={formData.role} \n                  onChange={(e) => className=\"user-manager-footer\">\n            {selectedUserId && selectedUserId !== currentUser.id && (\n              <button className=\"delete-button\" onClick={handleDelete}>{t('Delete')}</button>\n            )}\n            <div className=\"footer-right\">\n              <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n              <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleSave}>{t('Save')}</button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        )}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",

  }

       value={formData.password} \n                    onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, password: e.currentTarget.value })}\n                  />\n                </div>\n              )}\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('Role')}</label>\n                <select \n                  value={formData.role} \n                  onChange={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, role: e.currentTarget.value as UserRole })}\n                >\n                  <option value=\"ADMIN\">ADMIN</option>\n                  <option value=\"TEACHER\">TEACHER</option>\n                  <option value=\"STUDENT\">STUDENT</option>\n                </select>\n              </div>\n\n              {selectedUserId && (\n                <button \n                  className=\"secondary-button\" \n                  onClick={() => setResetPasswordMode(true)}\n                >\n                  {t('Reset Password')}\n                </button>\n              )}\n            </div>\n          ) : (\n            <div className=\"user-form\">\n              <h3>{t('Reset Password')}</h3>\n              <p>{t('Resetting password for')}: {formData.email}</p>\n              <div className=\"form-group\">\n                <label>{t('New Password')}</label>\n                <input \n                  type=\"password\" \n                  value={newPassword} \n                  onInput={(e) => setNewPassword(e.currentTarget.value)}\n                />\n              </div>\n              <div className=\"form-actions\">\n                <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={() => setResetPasswordMode(false)}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n                <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleResetPassword}>{t('Reset')}</button>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          )}\n        </div>\n\n        {!resetPasswordMode && (\n          <div className=\"user-manager-footer\">\n            {selectedUserId && selectedUserId !== currentUser.id && (\n              <button className=\"delete-button\" onClick={handleDelete}>{t('Delete')}</button>\n            )}\n            <div className=\"footer-right\">\n              <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n              <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleSave}>{t('Save')}</button>\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        )}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I'll create `ProfileManager.tsx` for users to change their passwords. I'll include a simple form for current and new passwords, matching the styling of other managers, and ensure it correctly calls the `change-password` endpoint. I'll also add a CSS file later.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "file_path": "src/components/ProfileManager.tsx",
    "content": "import { useState } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { User } from '../types';\nimport './ProfileManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  user: User;\n}\n\nexport function ProfileManager({ backendUrl, onClose, user }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({\n    currentPassword: '',\n    newPassword: '',\n    confirmPassword: ''\n  });\n\n  const handleChangePassword = async () => {\n    if (!formData.currentPassword || !formData.newPassword) {\n      alert(t('Please fill in all required fields'));\n      return;\n    }\n    if (formData.newPassword !== formData.confirmPassword) {\n      alert(t('Passwords do not match'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/auth/change-password`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          currentPassword: formData.currentPassword,\n          newPassword: formData.newPassword\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        alert(t('Password changed successfully'));\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        const errData = await res.json();\n        alert(errData.error || t('Failed to change password'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error changing password:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"profile-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"profile-manager-box\">\n        <div className=\"profile-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('My Profile')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"profile-manager-content\">\n          <div className=\"user-info-section\">\n            <p><strong>{t('Email')}:</strong> {user.email}</p>\n            <p><strong>{t('Role')}:</strong> {user.role}</p>\n          </div>\n\n          <div className=\"password-change-section\">\n            <h3>{t('Change Password')}</h3>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Current Password')}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"password\" \n                value={formData.currentPassword} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, currentPassword: e.currentTarget.value })}\n              />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('New Password')}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"password\" \n                value={formData.newPassword} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, newPassword: e.currentTarget.value })}\n              />\n            </div>\n            <div className=\"form-group\">\n              <label>{t('Confirm New Password')}</label>\n              <input \n                type=\"password\" \n                value={formData.confirmPassword} \n                onInput={(e) => setFormData({ ...formData, confirmPassword: e.currentTarget.value })}\n              />\n            </div>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"profile-manager-footer\">\n          <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n          <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleChangePassword}>{t('Change Password')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

## MODEL ✨

I'll create `SystemSettingManager.tsx` and its CSS to allow admins to toggle public signup. I'll include a simple checkbox for `allowPublicSignup` and ensure it correctly handles fetching and saving the settings via the backend API. I'll also add a CSS file later.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport './SystemSettingManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n}\n\nexport function SystemSettingManager({ backendUrl, onClose }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [allowPublicSignup, setAllowPublicSignup] = useState(true);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchSettings = async () => {\n      try {\n        const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/settings`);\n        if (res.ok) {\n          const data = await res.json();\n          setAllowPublicSignup(data.allowPublicSignup);\n        }\n      } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Failed to fetch settings:', err);\n      }\n    };\n    fetchSettings();\n  }, []);\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/settings`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ allowPublicSignup })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        alert(t('Settings saved successfully'));\n        onClose();\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to save settings'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving settings:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"system-setting-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"system-setting-box\">\n        <div className=\"system-setting-header\">\n          <h2>{t('System Settings')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"system-setting-content\">\n          <div className=\"setting-item\">\n            <label className=\"checkbox-label\">\n              <input \n                type=\"checkbox\" \n                checked={allowPublicSignup} \n                onChange={(e) => setAllowPublicSignup(e.currentTarget.checked)}\n              />\n              {t('Allow Public Signup')}\n            </label>\n            <p className=\"setting-description\">\n              {t('If enabled, anyone can create an account from the login page.')}\n            </p>\n          </div>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"system-setting-footer\">\n          <button className=\"cancel-button\" onClick={onClose}>{t('Cancel')}</button>\n          <button className=\"save-button\" onClick={handleSave}>{t('Save Changes')}</button>\n        </div>\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n",
    "file_path": "src/components/SystemSettingManager.tsx"
  }
}
```

## USER 🧑‍💻

**Tool Response**:
```json
{
  "id": "write_file_1775364498006_0",

{
  "name": "replace",
  "args": {
    "new_string": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport './Login.css';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\n\ninterface Props {\n  onLogin: (email: string, pass: string) => void;\n  error?: string;\n  backendUrl: string;\n}\n\nexport function Login({ onLogin, error: loginError, backendUrl }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [isSignup, setIsSignup] = useState(false);\n  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');\n  const [password, setPassword] = useState('');\n  const [confirmPassword, setConfirmPassword] = useState('');\n  const [allowPublicSignup, setAllowPublicSignup] = useState(false);\n  const [error, setError] = useState<string | undefined>(loginError);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    setError(loginError);\n  }, [loginError]);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    const fetchSettings = async () => {\n      try {\n        const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/settings`);\n        if (res.ok) {\n          const data = fetchSettings();\n  }, [backendUrl]);\n\n  const handleSubmit = async (e: Event) => {\n    e.preventDefault();\n    setError(undefined);\n\n    if (isSignup) {\n      if (password !== confirmPassword) {\n        setError(t('Passwords do not match'));\n        return;\n      }\n\n      try {\n        const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/auth/register`, {\n          method: 'POST',\n          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n          body: JSON.stringify({ email, password })\n        });\n        if (res.ok) {\n          // サインアップ成功後、自動的にログイン\n          onLogin(email, failed'));\n      }\n    } else {\n      onLogin(email, password);\n    }\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"login-container\">\n      <div className=\"login-box\">\n        <h2>EduGrid Scheduler</h2>\n        <p>{isSignup ? t('Create your account') : t('Please sign in to continue')}</p>\n        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>\n          <div className=\"form-group\">\n className=\"login-error\">{error}</div>}\n          <button type=\"submit\" className=\"login-button\">\n            {isSignup ? t('Sign Up') : t('Sign In')}\n          </button>\n        </form>\n\n        {!isSignup && allowPublicSignup && (\n          <div className=\"signup-link\">\n            <span>{t('Don\\'t have an account?')}</span>\n            <button className=\"link-button\" ## MODEL ✨

I'll rewrite the entire `UserManager.tsx` file to avoid any potential `replace` tool issues, as the logic changes are significant. I'll include the new list-first view with searching and actions.**Tool Command**:
```json
{
  "name": "write_file",
  "args": {
    "content": "import { useState, useEffect } from 'preact/hooks';\nimport { useTranslation } from 'react-i18next';\nimport { User, UserRole } from '../types';\nimport './UserManager.css';\n\ninterface Props {\n  backendUrl: string;\n  onClose: () => void;\n  currentUser: User;\n}\n\nexport function UserManager({ backendUrl, onClose, currentUser }: Props) {\n  const { t } = useTranslation();\n  const [users, setUsers] = useState<User[]>([]);\n  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');\n  const [editingUserId, setEditingUserId] = useState<string | null>(null);\n  const [isAddingNew, setIsAddingNew] = useState(false);\n  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({\n    email: '',\n    password: '',\n    role: 'STUDENT' as UserRole\n  });\n  const [resetPasswordMode, setResetPasswordMode] = useState(false);\n  const [newPassword, setNewPassword] = useState('');\n\n  const fetchUsers = async () => {\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users`, { credentials: 'include' });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        const data = await res.json();\n        setUsers(data);\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Failed to fetch users:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    fetchUsers();\n  }, []);\n\n  useEffect(() => {\n    if (editingUserId && editingUserId !== 'new') {\n      const user = users.find(u => u.id === editingUserId);\n      if (user) {\n        setFormData({\n          email: user.email,\n          password: '',\n          role: user.role\n        });\n      }\n    } else {\n      setFormData({\n        email: '',\n        password: '',\n        role: 'STUDENT'\n      });\n    }\n    setResetPasswordMode(false);\n  }, [editingUserId, users]);\n\n  const handleSave = async () => {\n    if (!formData.email || (isAddingNew && !formData.password)) {\n      alert(t('Please fill in all required fields'));\n      return;\n    }\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          id: isAddingNew ? null : editingUserId,\n          ...formData\n        })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        fetchUsers();\n        setEditingUserId(null);\n        setIsAddingNew(false);\n        alert(t('User saved successfully'));\n      } else {\n        const errData = await res.json();\n        alert(errData.error || t('Failed to save user'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error saving user:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleDelete = async (id: string) => {\n    if (id === currentUser.id) {\n      alert(t('Cannot delete yourself'));\n      return;\n    }\n    if (!confirm(t('Are you sure you want to delete this user?'))) return;\n\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users/${id}`, {\n        method: 'DELETE',\n        credentials: 'include'\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        fetchUsers();\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to delete user'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error deleting user:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const handleResetPassword = async () => {\n    if (!editingUserId || !newPassword) return;\n    try {\n      const res = await fetch(`${backendUrl}/users/${editingUserId}/reset-password`, {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n        credentials: 'include',\n        body: JSON.stringify({ newPassword })\n      });\n      if (res.ok) {\n        setResetPasswordMode(false);\n        setNewPassword('');\n        setEditingUserId(null);\n        alert(t('Password reset successfully'));\n      } else {\n        alert(t('Failed to reset password'));\n      }\n    } catch (err) {\n      console.error('Error resetting password:', err);\n    }\n  };\n\n  const filteredUsers = users.filter(u => \n    u.email.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||\n    u.role.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase())\n  );\n\n  const startEdit = (user: User) => {\n    setEditingUserId(user.id);\n    setIsAddingNew(false);\n  };\n\n  const startReset = (user: User) => {\n    setEditingUserId(user.id);\n    setResetPasswordMode(true);\n  };\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"user-manager-overlay\">\n      <div className=\"user-manager-box larger\">\n        <div className=\"user-manager-header\">\n          <h2>{t('Manage Users')}</h2>\n          <button className=\"close-button\" onClick={onClose}>×</button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div className=\"user-manager-content\">\n          {!editingUserId && !isAddingNew ? t(res.name) : id;\n  };\n\n  const currentViewStart = startOfDay(baseDate);\n\n  const getHoliday = (date: Date) => {\n    const target = startOfDay(date);\n    return holidays.find(h => {\n      if (h.date) return isSameDay(target, startOfDay(parseISO(h.date)));\n      if (h.start && h.end) {\n        const start = startOfDay(parseISO(h.start));\n        const end = startOfDay(parseISO(h.end));\n        return (isSameDay(target, start) || isAfter(target, start)) && \n               (isSameDay(target, end) || isBefore(target, end));\n      }\n      return false;\n    });\n  };\n\n  const getDayCount = () => {\n    if (viewType === 'day') return 1;\n    if (viewType === 'week') return 7;\n    if (viewType === 'month') return 30;\n    if (viewType === 'year') {\n      const start = new Date(getYear(baseDate), 3, 1);\n      const end = new Date(getYear(baseDate) + 1, 2, 31);\n      return differenceInDays(end, start) + 1;\n    }\n    return 1;\n  };\n\n  const dayCount = getDayCount();\n  const displayDates = Array.from({ length: dayCount }).map((_, i) => addDays(currentViewStart, i));\n  const currentViewEnd = startOfDay(displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]);\n\n  const filteredResources = resources\n    .filter(r => r.type === viewMode)\n    .sort((a, b) => (a.order ?? periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: 3 }}\n           onDblClick={() => onEmptyEventClick?.(dateStr, p.id)} />\n    ));\n  });\n\n  // 行内での重なりを計算する汎用関数\n  const calculateLayout = (items: { id: string, start: number, end: number }[]) => {\n    if (items.length === 0) return [];\n    const placements: { id: string, start: number, end: number, level: number, maxLevelInGroup: number }[] = [];\n    const sortedItems = [...items].sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start || (b.end - b.start) - (a.end - a.start));\n    sortedItems.forEach(item => {\n      let level = 0;\n      while (placements.some(p => p.level === level && !(item.end < p.start || item.start > p.end))) {\n        level++;\n      }\n      placements.push({ ...item, level, maxLevelInGroup: 0 });\n    });\n    placements.forEach(p => {\n      const overlapping = placements.filter(other => !(p.end < other.start || p.start > other.end));\n      p.maxLevelInGroup = Math.max(...overlapping.map(o => o.level)) + 1;\n    });\n    return placements;\n  };\n\n  // --- 行事行（row 3）のデータ準備 ---\n  const row3Items: { id: string, start: number, end: number, type: 'holiday' | 'event', data: any }[] = [];\n  displayDates.forEach((date, dIdx) => {\n    const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n    if (!holiday) return;\n    if (holiday.date && isSameDay(date, startOfDay(parseISO(holiday.date)))) {\n      const startCol = dIdx * periods.length + 2;\n      const endCol = dIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 2;\n      row3Items.push({ id: `holiday-${date.toISOString()}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, type: 'holiday', data: holiday });\n    } (isSameDay(date, displayDates[0]) && isAfter(date, hStart) && isBefore(date, hEnd))) {\n        const actualStart = isAfter(hStart, displayDates[0]) ? hStart : displayDates[0];\n        const actualEnd = isBefore(hEnd, displayDates[displayDates.length - 1]) ? hEnd : displayDates[displayDates.length - 1];\n        const sIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualStart));\n        const eIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, actualEnd));\n        if (sIdx !== -1 && eIdx !== -1 && isSameDay(date, actualStart)) {\n          const startCol = sIdx * periods.length + 2;\n          const endCol = eIdx * periods.length + periods.length + 2;\n          row3Items.push({ id: `holiday-range-${holiday.name}-${date.toISOString()}`, start: startCol, end: endCol - 1, type: 'holiday', data: holiday });\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  });\n\n  events.forEach(e => {\n    const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate));\n    const eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n      const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n      row3Items.push({ id: `event-${e.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, type: 'event', data: e });\n    }\n  });\n\n  const row3Layouts = calculateLayout(row3Items);\n  const holidayItems = row3Layouts.filter(l => row3Items.find(i => i.id === l.id)?.type === 'holiday').map(layout => {\n    const item = row3Items.find(i => i.id === layout.id)!;\n    const h = item.data;\n    const unitHeight = (80 - 8) / layout.maxLevelInGroup;\n    const itemHeight = unitHeight - 8;\n    const top = 70 + 4 + (layout.level * unitHeight);\n    return (\n      <div key={layout.id} className=\"event-card holiday-card\"\n           title={h.name}\n           style={{ gridColumn: `${layout.start} / ${layout.end + 1}`, gridRow: 3, top: `${top}px`, height: `${itemHeight}px` }}>\n        {h.name}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  const globalEventItems = row3Layouts.filter(l => row3Items.find(i => i.id === l.id)?.type === 'event').map(layout => {\n    const e = row3Items.find(i => i.id === layout.id)!.data as ScheduleEvent;\n    const unitHeight = (80 - 8) / layout.maxLevelInGroup;\n    const itemHeight = unitHeight - 8;\n    const top = 70 + 4 + (layout.level * unitHeight);\n\n    const startP = periods.find(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId)?.name || e.startPeriodId;\n    const endP = periods.find(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId)?.name || e.endPeriodId;\n    const resNames = [\n      ...(e.resourceIds || []),\n      ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)\n    ].map(id => getResourceName(id)).join(', ');\n\n    const tooltip = `${e.name}\\n${e.startDate} ${startP} ～ ${e.endDate} ${endP}` + (resNames ? `\\n${labels.event}: ${resNames}` : '');\n\n    return (\n      <div key={layout.id} className=\"event-card schedule-event-card\"\n           title={tooltip}\n           style={{ gridColumn: `${layout.start} / ${layout.end + 1}`, gridRow: 3, backgroundColor: e.color, top: `${top}px`, height: `${itemHeight}px`, cursor: 'pointer' }}\n           onDblClick={() => onEventClick?.(e)}>\n        {e.name}\n      </div>\n    );\n  });\n\n  // --- リソース行のデータ準備 ---\n  const resourceEventItems: JSX.Element[] = [];\n  filteredResources.forEach((res, resIdx) => {\n    const resItems: { id: string, start: number, end: number, data: ScheduleEvent }[] = [];\n    events.forEach(e => {\n      const resourceIdList = [...(e.resourceIds || []), ...(e.resources || []).map(r => r.id)];\n      if (resourceIdList.includes(res.id)) {\n        const eStart = startOfDay(parseISO(e.startDate));\n        const eEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(e.endDate));\n        if (isAfter(eStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(eEnd, currentViewStart)) return;\n        const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eStart));\n        const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, eEnd));\n        const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId);\n        const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId);\n        const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n        const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n        resItems.push({ id: `event-${e.id}-${res.id}`, start: sCol, end: eCol, data: e });\n      }\n    });\n\n    const layouts = calculateLayout(resItems);\n    layouts.forEach(layout => {\n      const e = resItems.find(i => i.id === layout.id)!.data;\n      const unitHeight = (80 - 8) / layout.maxLevelInGroup;\n      const itemHeight = unitHeight - 8;\n      const top = 4 + (layout.level * unitHeight);\n\n      const startP = periods.find(p => p.id === e.startPeriodId)?.name || e.startPeriodId;\n      const endP = periods.find(p => p.id === e.endPeriodId)?.name || e.endPeriodId;\n      const tooltip = `${e.name}\\n${e.startDate} ${startP} ～ ${e.endDate} ${endP}`;\n\n      resourceEventItems.push(\n        <div key={layout.id} className=\"event-card schedule-event-card resource-event-card\"\n             title={tooltip}\n             style={{ gridColumn: `${layout.start} / ${layout.end + 1}`, gridRow: resIdx + 4, backgroundColor: e.color, top: `${top}px`, height: `${itemHeight}px`, cursor: 'pointer', position: 'relative' }}\n             onDblClick={() => onEventClick?.(e)}>\n          {e.name}\n        </div>\n      );\n    });\n  });\n\n  const resourceLabels = filteredResources.map((r, idx) => (\n    <div key={`label-${r.id}`} className=\"grid-label\" style={{ ...stickyLeft, gridColumn: 1, gridRow: idx + 4 }}>\n      {t(r.name)}\n    </div>\n  ));\n\n  const lessonItems = lessons.flatMap(l => {\n    const lStart = startOfDay(parseISO(l.startDate));\n    const lEnd = startOfDay(parseISO(l.endDate));\n    if (isAfter(lStart, currentViewEnd) || isBefore(lEnd, currentViewStart)) return [];\n\n    const startDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lStart));\n    const endDayIdx = displayDates.findIndex(d => isSameDay(d, lEnd));\n    const startPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.startPeriodId);\n    const endPeriodIdx = periods.findIndex(p => p.id === l.endPeriodId);\n    const sCol = (startDayIdx === -1) ? 2 : startDayIdx * periods.length + startPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const eCol = (endDayIdx === -1) ? (displayDates.length * periods.length + 1) : endDayIdx * periods.length + endPeriodIdx + 2;\n    const span = eCol - sCol + 1;\n    const subIds = [\n      ...(l.subTeacherIds || []),\n      ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)\n    ];\n    // 関連するリソースIDを特定\n    let targetResIds: string[] = [];\n    if (viewMode === 'room' && l.roomId) targetResIds = [l.roomId];\n    else if (viewMode === 'teacher') {\n      const allTeacherIds = [];\n      if (l.teacherId) allTeacherIds.push(l.teacherId);\n      if (subIds.length > 0) allTeacherIds.push(...subIds);\n      targetResIds = allTeacherIds;\n    }\n    else if (viewMode === 'course') targetResIds = [l.courseId];\n\n    return targetResIds.map(resId => {\n      const resourceIdx = filteredResources.findIndex(r => r.id === resId);\n      if (resourceIdx === -1) return null;\n      const infoItems = [];\n\n      const currentCourse = resources.find(c => c.id === l.courseId);\n      const mainTeacherLabel = labels.mainTeacher;\n      const subTeacherLabel = labels.subTeacher;\n\n      const roomValue = l.roomId ? getResourceName(l.roomId) : (l.location || t('No room'));\n      if (viewMode !== 'room') infoItems.push({ label: labels.room, value: roomValue });\n\n      const mainTeacherName = l.teacherId ? getResourceName(l.teacherId) : t('No main teacher');\n      const subIds = [\n        ...(l.subTeacherIds || []),\n        ...(l.subTeachers || []).map(t => t.id)\n      ];\n      const subTeacherNames = subIds.map(id => getResourceName(id));\n\n      if (viewMode !== 'teacher') {\n        if (l.teacherId) infoItems.push({ label: mainTeacherLabel, value: mainTeacherName });\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) infoItems.push({ label: subTeacherLabel, value: subTeacherNames.join(', ') });\n      } else {\n        // 講師ビューの場合は、全講師（自分含む）を併記するがラベルはどうするか？\n        // 講師ビューではシンプルに「講師」ラベルまたは個別の役割を表示\n        if (l.teacherId) infoItems.push({ label: mainTeacherLabel, value: mainTeacherName });\n        if (subTeacherNames.length > 0) infoItems.push({ label: subTeacherLabel, value: subTeacherNames.join(', ') });\n      }\n      if (viewMode !== 'course') infoItems.push({ label: labels.course, value: getResourceName(l.courseId) });\n\n      const translatedSubject = t(l.subject);\n      const tooltipText = `${translatedSubject}\\n` + \n                         (l.location ? '#e884fa' : undefined \n          }}\n          title={tooltipText}\n          onDblClick={() => onLessonClick?.(l)}\n        >\n          <div className=\"lesson-subject\">{translatedSubject}</div>\n          <div className=\"lesson-details\">\n            {infoItems.map((item, idx) => (\n              <div key={idx} className=\"lesson-info\">\n                {item.label}: {item.value}\n              </div>\n            ))}\n          </div>\n        </div>\n      );\n    }).filter(Boolean);\n  });\n\n  const wrapperStyle = {\n    overflowX: isDayView ? 'hidden' : 'auto'\n  } as JSX.CSSProperties;\n\n  return (\n    <div className=\"timetable-wrapper\" style={wrapperStyle}>\n      <div \n        key={`grid-${viewType}-${baseDate.getTime()}-${viewMode}-${filteredResources.length}-${totalCols}`}\n        className=\"timetable-container\" \n        style={gridStyle}\n      >\n        <div className=\"grid-corner\" style={{ ...stickyLeft, gridColumn: 1, gridRow: \"1 / span 2\", zIndex: 100 }} />\n        {filteredResources.map((res, rIdx) => \n          displayDates.map((date, dIdx) => {\n            const isSun = date.getDay() === 0;\n            const isSat = date.getDay() === 6;\n            const holiday = getHoliday(date);\n            const dateStr = format(date, 'yyyy-MM-dd');\n            let cellClass = 'grid-cell';\n            if (isSun) cellClass += ' is-sunday';\n            if (isSat) cellClass += ' is-saturday';\n            if (holiday) cellClass += ' is-holiday';\n            return periods.map((p, pIdx) => (\n              <div key={`cell-${rIdx}-${dIdx}-${pIdx}`} \n                   className={cellClass} \n                   style={{ gridColumn: dIdx * periods.length + pIdx + 2, gridRow: rIdx + 4 }}\n                   onDblClick={() => onEmptyResourceCellClick?.(res.id, dateStr, p.id)} />\n            ));\n          })\n        )}\n        {dateHeaders}\n        {periodHeaders}\n        {eventLabel}\n        {eventCells}\n        {/* レベル別の配置を確保 */}\n        {holidayItems}\n        {globalEventItems}\n        {resourceEventItems}\n        {resourceLabels}\n        {lessonItems}\n      </div>\n    </div>\n  );\n}\n"
  }
}
```

---

## MODEL ✨

I'll refactor `Timetable.tsx` to handle overlapping lessons and events within resource rows. I'll consolidate `ScheduleEvents` and `Lessons` into a single list per resource, use the `calculateLayout` function to determine their levels and maximum overlap, and then render them with adjusted heights and vertical positions. I'll also ensure that `ScheduleEvent` items include all necessary data for rendering and tooltips. First, I'll identify and prepare the items for each resource row.**Tool Command**:
```json
